class="operation-target inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 p-1.5 no-underline hover:text-tertiary" href="https://github.com/Stedi/openApi/blob/main/manager.json#:~:text=&quot;operationId&quot;%3A%20&quot;GetBatchItems&quot;" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon text-tertiary"><path d="M4 18V14.3C4 13.4716 3.32843 12.8 2.5 12.8H2V11.2H2.5C3.32843 11.2 4 10.5284 4 9.7V6C4 4.34315 5.34315 3 7 3H8V5H7C6.44772 5 6 5.44772 6 6V10.1C6 10.9858 5.42408 11.7372 4.62623 12C5.42408 12.2628 6 13.0142 6 13.9V18C6 18.5523 6.44772 19 7 19H8V21H7C5.34315 21 4 19.6569 4 18ZM20 14.3V18C20 19.6569 18.6569 21 17 21H16V19H17C17.5523 19 18 18.5523 18 18V13.9C18 13.0142 18.5759 12.2628 19.3738 12C18.5759 11.7372 18 10.9858 18 10.1V6C18 5.44772 17.5523 5 17 5H16V3H17C18.6569 3 20 4.34315 20 6V9.7C20 10.5284 20.6716 11.2 21.5 11.2H22V12.8H21.5C20.6716 12.8 20 13.4716 20 14.3Z"></path></svg>OpenAPI spec</a></div></div></div><p>This endpoint retrieves the processing status and other summary information for all of the eligibility checks in the specified batch. It doesn&#x27;t include the complete eligibility response. For the full results of each eligibility check, call the <a href="/docs/healthcare/api-reference/get-healthcare-polling-eligibility">Poll Batch Checks</a> endpoint instead.</p>
<p>You can use this endpoint to determine whether specific eligibility checks within a batch have completed. You can also use the response to determine whether patients have active or inactive coverage without having to poll.</p>
<ol>
<li>Call this endpoint with the batch ID for the eligibility check batch. This is the <code>batchId</code> Stedi returned in the <a href="/docs/healthcare/api-reference/post-healthcare-batch-eligibility">Batch Eligibility Checks</a> endpoint response. It&#x27;s also available on the batch&#x27;s details page in the Stedi portal.</li>
<li>Stedi returns information about the processing status of each eligibility check within the batch, including whether the check completed successfully and information about the patient&#x27;s coverage status (<code>eligibilitySearchStatus</code>). Each <code>item</code> in the response corresponds to one eligibility check within the batch.</li>

leading-[24px]"><p>A list of batch items. Each <code>item</code> represents a single eligibility check in the batch. Unlike the polling endpoint, which only returns results for completed eligibility checks, this endpoint returns results for all eligibility checks in the batch, regardless of their processing status.</p>
<p>All batch items may not be returned in a single response; use the <code>nextPageToken</code> to retrieve subsequent pages of results.</p><details dark:bg-blue-950/50 text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-300 break-all whitespace-normal inline-flex items-center gap-1"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon size-3.5"><path d="M3 4H21V6H3V4ZM3 19H17V21H3V19ZM3 14H21V16H3V14ZM3 9H17V11H3V9Z"></path></svg>String</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The status of the eligibility check. Can be:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>queued</code>: Stedi placed the eligibility check in its internal queue and will send it to the payer when resources are available. This status is common when you schedule batch eligibility check refreshes through the API or perform large bulk retries that exceed your account&#x27;s concurrency budget. You can typically expect the status to change to <code>Started</code> within a few seconds.</li>
<li><code>started</code>: Stedi has sent the eligibility check to the payer and is waiting for a response.</li>
<li><code>failed</code>: The payer returned an error code in the response. Review the error code and retry the eligibility check.</li>
<li><code>inactive</code>: The payer&#x27;s response doesn&#x27;t contain an active eligibility and benefit type. This means that the patient doesn&#x27;t have active coverage for the requested services.</li>
<li><code>active</code>: The payer&#x27;s response contains an active eligibility and benefit type. This means that the patient has active coverage for at least some services.</li>
</ul><div><section class="rounded-md border bg-fd-card"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between p-3 border-t border-b first:border-t-0 last:rounded-b-md first:rounded-t-md"><div aria-level="1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon size-3.5"><path d="M3 4H21V6H3V4ZM3 19H17V21H3V19ZM3 14H21V16H3V14ZM3 9H17V11H3V9Z"></path></svg>String</span><span class="px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md font-[500] text-[13px] bg-red-50 dark:bg-red-950/50 text-red-700 dark:text-red-300 whitespace-nowrap break-all" data-component-part="field-required-pill">Required</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The current state of the eligibility check. Can be:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>PENDING</code>: Stedi hasn&#x27;t begun processing the eligibility check.</li>
<li><code>VALIDATED</code>: Stedi finished validating the eligibility check and is ready to execute it.</li>
<li><code>VALIDATION_FAILED</code>: Stedi found errors in the eligibility check that you need to fix before processing can continue. This is typically due to malformed CSV data, missing required fields, or invalid values.</li>
<li><code>STARTED</code>: Stedi has begun processing the eligibility check.</li>
<li><code>RETRYING</code>: Stedi is retrying the eligibility check. Stedi retries eligibility checks that fail due to payer connectivity issues for up to 8 hours.</li>
<li><code>COMPLETED</code>: Stedi successfully processed the eligibility check and received a response from the payer. This doesn&#x27;t indicate that the payer has active coverage, only that Stedi was able to get a response.</li>
<li><code>COMPLETED_WITH_ERRORS</code>: Stedi finished processing the eligibility check, but couldn&#x27;t get a response from the payer. A common reason for failure is payer connectivity issues.</li>
</ul><div><section class="rounded-md border bg-fd-card"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between p-3 border-t border-b first:border-t-0 last:rounded-b-md first:rounded-t-md"><div aria-level="1" current state of the eligibility check. Can be:\n  - `PENDING`: Stedi hasn't begun processing the eligibility check.\n  - `VALIDATED`: Stedi finished validating the eligibility check and is ready to execute it.\n  - `VALIDATION_FAILED`: Stedi found errors in the eligibility check that you need to fix before processing can continue. This is typically due to malformed CSV data, missing required fields, or invalid values.\n  - `STARTED`: Stedi has begun processing the eligibility check.\n  - `RETRYING`: Stedi is retrying the eligibility check. Stedi retries eligibility checks that fail due to payer connectivity issues for up to 8 hours.\n  - `COMPLETED`: Stedi successfully processed the eligibility check and received a response from the payer. This doesn't indicate that the payer has active coverage, only that Stedi was able to get a response.\n  - `COMPLETED_WITH_ERRORS`: Stedi finished processing the eligibility check, but couldn't get a response from the payer. A common reason for failure is payer connectivity issues."])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"58:[\"$\",\"$L47\",\"application/json\",{\"value\":\"application/json\",\"children\":[null,[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"my-2\",\"children\":[[[\"$\",\"$1\",\"items\",{\"children\":[\"$\",\"$L48\",null,{\"constraints\":{\"default\":\"$undefined\",\"pattern\":\"$undefined\",\"format\":\"$undefined\",\"multipleOf\":\"$undefined\",\"minimum\":\"$undefined\",\"exclusiveMinimum\":\"$undefined\",\"maximum\":\"$undefined\",\"exclusiveMaximum\":\"$undefined\",\"minLength\":\"$undefined\",\"maxLength\":\"$undefined\",\"minProperties\":\"$undefined\",\"maxProperties\":\"$undefined\",\"minItems\":\"$undefined\",\"maxItems\":\"$undefined\"},\"deprecated\":\"$undefined\",\"name\":\"items\",\"namespace\":\"response\",\"schema\":{\"description\":\"A list of batch items.
